### [88] [Interplay of Holographic and New Agegraphic Dark Energy in Cosmology: A hybrid dark energy model from a generalized length-time cut-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23728)
*Sayani Maity,Aritra Sanyal,Prabir Rudra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文受广义相对论时空统一启发，提出了一种结合Holographic暗能量(HDE)和新Agegraphic暗能量(NADE)的混合暗能量模型，其中能量密度由空间和时间两种截断共同决定。研究了该模型与冷暗物质的相互作用和非相互作用情形，通过状态方程参数、减速参数、Statefinder参数和Om诊断等分析了宇宙学含义，利用声速平方进行了稳定性检验，并用Hubble、BAO和DESI观测数据约束了参数空间。结果表明该混合模型能成功描述宇宙演化，且Hubble张力显著低于其他模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HDE和NADE模型分别单独采用空间和时间红外截断来定义暗能量密度，但广义相对论表明时空是统一的。因此，有必要提出一个同时考虑空间和时间截断的混合模型，使HDE和NADE作为极端情形出现，从而更完整地描述暗能量。

Method: 构建HDE和NADE能量密度线性组合的混合暗能量模型；分别考虑与冷暗物质有相互作用和无相互作用的两种场景；通过状态方程参数w、减速参数q、Statefinder参数(r,s)和Om诊断进行宇宙学分析；使用声速平方进行稳定性检验；利用Hubble、BAO和DESI观测数据进行参数空间约束；评估模型对Hubble张力的缓解程度。

Result: 该混合模型能够成功描述宇宙演化；Hubble张力相比其他模型显著降低；观测数据对参数空间给出了有效约束；模型通过了稳定性检验。

Conclusion: 所构建的时空截断混合暗能量模型是一个有效的暗能量候选模型，能统一HDE和NADE，且对Hubble张力问题有较好的缓解能力。

Abstract: The spatial and temporal infrared cutoffs are the source of the Holographic dark energy (HDE) and New Agegraphic dark energy (NADE) models, respectively. Inspired by the spacetime unification of space and time in General Relativity, we propose that a combined spacetime cutoff should govern the dark energy density, with HDE and NADE appearing as limiting cases when the spatial or temporal contribution predominates. In this connection, we explore a hybrid model of holographic and new Agegraphic dark energy, where the energy density of the resulting model is a combination of the two models. We consider an interacting and a non-interacting scenario between the hybrid dark energy model and cold dark matter. Cosmological implications of the model is studied via different cosmological parameters like the equation of state parameter, deceleration parameter, statefinder parameter, and Om-diagnostic. A stability check for the model has been performed using the squared speed of sound. Finally the parameter space of the model is constrained using observational data like Hubble data, BAO data and DESI data. We have also checked the Hubble tension for our hybrid model and found it to be substantially low in comparison to other models. From our analysis we see that the constructed hybrid dark energy model can describe the evolution of the universe successfully.

</details>


### [89] [Potentially healthy time evolution in interacting $p$-form fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23731)
*Fethi M. Ramazanoğlu,Kıvanç İ. Ünlütürk*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了p-形式场的自相互作用在时间演化中的双曲性丧失问题。在4维时空中，3-形式场与矢量场（1-形式）类似，可以通过特定自相互作用项保持健康的时间演化；而2-形式场则仍然存在双曲性丧失问题。此外，消除质量项的方法并不能解决该问题，而是将奇点转移到运动方程的其他部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近发现许多自相互作用矢量场在场振幅较小时具有健康的时间演化，但当场的范数达到某个有限值时动力学变得不可能。这一结果也被推广到更高阶形式场。然而，最近的另一项工作表明，某些特定自相互作用的矢量场理论可以避免此类问题。本文旨在研究p-形式场是否存在类似的例外情况，以及不同阶形式场在自相互作用下的双曲性差异。

Method: 在4维时空中，分别对1-形式（矢量场）、2-形式场和3-形式场的自相互作用进行双曲性分析，比较不同阶形式场在自相互作用下的时间演化行为，并分析消除质量项方案的有效性。

Result: 3-形式场的自相互作用可以保持健康的时间演化，类似于矢量场的例外情况；2-形式场的自相互作用仍然导致双曲性丧失；消除质量项的方法将奇点转移到运动方程的其他部分，不能提供良定的时间演化。

Conclusion: 不同阶p-形式场在自相互作用下的双曲性行为存在本质差异：在4维时空中，1-形式和3-形式场可以存在健康的自相互作用理论，而2-形式场则不能。消除质量项的方案并不能真正解决问题。

Abstract: It was recently discovered that many self-interacting vector fields can have healthy time evolution when field amplitudes are small, however, further dynamics becomes impossible if the norm of the field reaches a certain finite value. This result was also generalized to higher form fields using the fact that vector fields can also be viewed as 1-form fields. However, other recent work demonstrated that some exceptional vector field theories do not suffer from such problems if the self-interaction term is chosen in a specific way. Here, we study whether a similar exception exists for $p$-form fields in general. We show that, in 4 spacetime dimensions, 3-form fields with self interaction can indeed have healthy time evolution similarly to vectors. However, the analogous coupling terms still lead to loss of hyperbolicity for 2-form fields. We study the reasons for these differences, and comment on directions to generalize our findings. We also demonstrate that eliminating the mass term, one of the proposals to build healthy self-interacting vector field theories, moves the singularity to other parts of the equations of motion, hence, most likely does not provide well-posed time evolution.

</details>


### [90] [Removing Ostrogradsky modes in multi-field higher-order scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23734)
*Hamed Bouzari Nezhad*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究多场高阶标量-张量理论中如何移除Ostrogradsky鬼模，推导了在度规动能块可逆分支下，主退化条件、反对称一致性条件以及秩条件共同确保理论传播2+𝒩个自由度（两个张量模加每个场一个标量模）的完整判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多场高阶标量-张量理论中，Ostrogradsky鬼模的存在导致理论不稳定，需要找到系统的退化条件来移除这些非物理自由度。单场情况已有成熟结果，但多场情形面临更复杂的场空间矩阵结构和额外的一致性条件，尚无完整分析。

Method: 对具有任意数量𝒩个标量场且对二阶导数呈二次依赖的理论，采用ADM分解并在度规动能块可逆的分支中进行哈密顿分析。推导出主退化条件（场空间矩阵条件）、守恒主退化约束产生的反对称一致性条件，以及约束代数的最终秩条件。

Result: 主退化条件在多场情形下不足以保证移除Ostrogradsky模，还需满足反对称一致性条件（在单场情形无对应物）和秩条件。满足这三条条件后，理论传播2+𝒩个自由度（两个张量模加每场一个标量模），无额外Ostrogradsky模。在单场极限、多场二次Horndeski子类以及一个显式退化多场子类中验证了构造有效性。

Conclusion: 建立了多场高阶标量-张量理论移除Ostrogradsky鬼模的完整哈密顿判据体系，识别了多场特有的反对称一致性条件，为构建稳定的多场引力理论提供了系统方法论。

Abstract: We study multi-field higher-order scalar-tensor theories and examine how the unwanted Ostrogradsky modes can be removed. For a general class of theories with an arbitrary number $\mathcal{N}$ of scalar fields and quadratic dependence on their second derivatives, we perform an ADM decomposition and develop the Hamiltonian analysis in the branch where the metric kinetic block is invertible. The primary degeneracy condition takes the form of a matrix condition in field space, but in a genuine multi-field theory it is not by itself sufficient: preserving the primary degeneracy constraints generates additional consistency conditions, some of which are antisymmetric in the field-space indices and have no direct analogue in the single-field case. Together with the primary degeneracy condition and a final rank condition on the constraint algebra, these conditions are sufficient for the theory to propagate $2+\mathcal{N}$ degrees of freedom, the two tensor modes of gravity together with one scalar mode per field, and no additional Ostrogradsky mode. We illustrate the construction in the single-field limit, in a multi-field quadratic Horndeski-type subclass, and in an explicit degenerate multi-field subclass that shows these conditions can be satisfied.

</details>


### [91] [Physical properties of charged black holes from the nonlinear electrodynamics model based on electric potential regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23746)
*S. Habib Mazharimousavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦引力与非线性电动力学（NED）耦合产生的静态球对称黑洞解，该NED模型由点电荷的正则化电势构建。时空由ADM质量M、电荷Q和非线性标度r₀三个参数刻画。结果表明，解展现出丰富的因果结构（单、双、三视界及裸奇点），中心奇点的性质由组合量m-⅔q²决定。热力学分析揭示了两个临界电荷参数：低于临界值时黑洞热不稳定，高于临界值时在有限范围内出现稳定相；足够大电荷时出现零温极端构型。观测特征方面，NED修正导致光子球可能消失，与RN解产生显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性电动力学修正下带电黑洞的因果结构、热力学相空间和可观测特征，揭示与标准Reissner-Nordström黑洞的差异。

Method: 通过构建正则化点电荷电势的NED模型，求解爱因斯坦场方程得到静态球对称黑洞解；利用霍金温度和热容进行热力学分析；通过零测地线分析研究黑洞阴影等观测特征。

Result: 1) 存在单、双、三视界及裸奇点等丰富因果结构；2) 发现两个临界电荷参数控制热行为，低于临界值不稳定，高于临界值出现稳定相；3) 极端构型（T=0）进一步约束稳定区域；4) 超过临界电荷时光子球可能消失，阴影产生可观测偏差。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学显著丰富了带电黑洞的因果结构、热力学相空间和动力学响应，提供了可观测的偏离RN范式的信号。

Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric black hole solutions arising from Einstein gravity minimally coupled to a nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) model constructed from a regularized electric potential of a point charge. The resulting spacetime is characterized by three parameters, namely, the ADM mass $% M $, the electric charge $Q$, and the nonlinear scale $r_{0}$. We show that, depending on the values of $M$ and $Q$, the solutions exhibit a rich causal structure comprising black holes with single, double, and triple horizons, as well as naked singular geometries. The nature of the central singularity is determined by the combination $m-\frac{2}{3}q^{2}$, allowing for both spacelike and timelike singularities. We perform a detailed thermodynamic analysis by deriving the Hawking temperature and heat capacity, revealing the existence of two critical charge parameters that govern the thermal behavior. Below a critical charge, the black holes are thermally unstable, whereas above it a stable phase emerges within a finite range of horizon radii bounded by Davies points. For sufficiently large charge, extremal configurations with vanishing temperature arise, further constraining the stability region. We also investigate observational signatures by analyzing null geodesics and black hole shadows, showing that nonlinear electrodynamics corrections lead to noticeable deviations from the Reissner-Nordström geometry, including the possible absence of a photon sphere beyond a critical charge. Our results highlight that nonlinear electrodynamics significantly enriches the causal structure, thermodynamic phase space, and dynamical response of charged black holes, providing potentially observable deviations from the Reissner-Nordström paradigm.

</details>

Method: 基于EGUP理论框架，计算Kerr-Newman五重态黑洞的霍金温度、热容、吉布斯自由能、熵和压强等热力学量，并与GUP和EUP的结果进行对比分析。

Result: 得到了EGUP修正下Kerr-Newman五重态黑洞的热力学量变化规律，揭示了从早期宇宙（GUP主导）到晚期宇宙（EUP主导）的热力学演化差异，并确定了剩余质量、温度和稳定性条件。

Conclusion: EGUP能够统一描述黑洞从早期到晚期宇宙的热力学行为，GUP和EUP分别适用于不同宇宙阶段，五重态暗能量对黑洞热力学性质有显著影响。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the effects of the Extended Generalized Uncertainty Principle (EGUP) on the thermodynamic quantities of the Kerr-Newman black hole surrounded by quintessence (KNBHQ). Additionally, we conduct a comparative analysis of the outcomes derived from the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) and the Extended Uncertainty Principle (EUP). The GUP is crucial in the context of the early universe, whereas the EUP is significant in the framework of the later universe. This analysis illustrates the variations in thermodynamic quantities, including Hawking temperature, heat capacity, Gibbs free energy, entropy and pressure of the Kerr-Newman black hole, as they evolve from the early universe to the latter universe under the influence of the dark energy model known as quintessence. The remnant mass, temperature and the stability of the KNBHQ are also studied.

We study the global structure including horizons and singularities, and derive the first law of black hole thermodynamics. The emergence of a cosmological horizon in Einstein-Maxwell gravity without invoking a positive cosmological constant or dark energy is tantalizing, and may provide a new avenue for exploring cosmological and astrophysical phenomena related to black holes and the late-time cosmology.

### [94] [Black Hole Ringdown Nonlinearities in the Large-D Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23804)
*Roberto Emparan,Amanda Green-Salinas,David Pereñiguez,Jaime Redondo-Yuste*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用大D极限下的有效理论研究了黑洞合并环down阶段的非线性效应，推导了静态黑洞被单准正规模式驱动的三阶响应解析表达式，并将其应用于非旋转黑洞对头碰撞的环down分析。结果表明，包含二次和三次非线性效应可将准正规模式建模的精度提高数个数量级，且非线性效应强度随碰撞速度增加而增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞环down研究主要基于线性微扰理论，非线性效应尚未被充分理解。作者希望利用大D极限有效理论在解析可解性和计算效率上的优势，系统研究黑洞合并环down阶段的非线性响应，填补这一理论空白。

Method: 采用大D极限下的黑洞动力学有效理论，该框架下准正规模式谱（含非线性修正）可解析求解；利用计算成本低的数值碰撞模拟；推导了静态黑洞被单一准正规模式驱动的三阶响应解析表达式，并将其应用于不同速度和质量比下的非旋转黑洞对头碰撞。

Result: 包含二次和三次非线性效应后，准正规模式建模的精度提高了数个数量级；非线性效应强度随碰撞速度增加而明显增强。

Conclusion: 大D极限有效理论为研究黑洞环down非线性效应提供了一个干净、可控且计算高效的框架；非线性效应对精确建模黑洞弛豫过程至关重要，尤其在高速碰撞情形下不可忽略。

Abstract: We initiate the study of nonlinear effects in the ringdown phase of black hole mergers using the effective theory of black hole dynamics in the large-D limit. This framework offers several advantages: the quasinormal mode spectrum, including nonlinear corrections, is analytically tractable; numerical simulations of collisions are computationally inexpensive; and the extraction and analysis of the ringdown signal are clean and controlled. As a proof of concept, we derive analytic expressions for the third-order response of a static black hole driven by a single quasinormal mode, and apply them to study the ringdown following head-on collisions of non-spinning black holes across a range of velocities and mass ratios. We find that including nonlinear effects, up to quadratic and cubic order, improves the accuracy of quasinormal-mode modelling of black hole relaxation by several orders of magnitude. The results also show a clear growth in the strength of nonlinear effects as the collision velocity increases.

</details>


### [95] [A thorough investigation of cross-correlation estimators for stochastic gravitational-wave background searches in ground-based detector data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23816)
*Haowen Zhong,Joseph D. Romano,Vuk Mandic,Shivaraj Kandhasamy,Arianna I. Renzini*

TL;DR: 本文系统性地重新审视并在频域中重新表述了用于随机引力波背景探测的交叉相关方法，明确解决并克服了时域中数据加窗和重叠导致的非零协方差问题；提出了新窄带估计量及其协方差表达式，并证明了以往广泛使用的表达式仍能给出正确的参数估计后验分布和模型选择的贝叶斯因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机引力波背景探测是引力波天文学的关键挑战，现有方法主要依赖时域宽带交叉相关估计量，但越来越多的分析需要精确的频域窄带估计量来刻画特定频率区间的能量密度；从时域宽带估计量到频域窄带估计量的过渡在现有文献中尚未被充分探索，存在显著复杂性。

Method: 系统性地在频域中重新审视并重新表述交叉相关方法，明确处理时域数据加窗和重叠引入的非零协方差问题；推导新的窄带估计量及其协方差表达式；并与以往广泛使用的表达式进行对比验证。

Result: 提出了新的窄带估计量及其协方差的表达式，这些表达式与过去搜索中使用的不同；但证明了以往使用的表达式在参数估计时仍能产生正确的后验分布，在模型选择时仍能产生正确的对数贝叶斯因子。

Conclusion: 建立了稳健的理论框架，有助于更准确且更具物理洞察力地解释随机引力波背景观测，为当前和未来的相关研究奠定了必要基础。

Abstract: Detecting a stochastic gravitational-wave background represents a crucial yet challenging objective within the field of gravitational-wave astronomy. Ground-based detectors currently rely almost exclusively on cross-correlation methods to detect stochastic gravitational-wave background signals. Traditionally, these methods define and optimize a broadband estimator initially constructed in the time domain. However, a growing number of analyses require precise narrowband estimators to accurately characterize the energy density of the underlying signal in specific frequency bins. Transitioning from time-domain broadband estimators to frequency-domain narrowband estimators introduces significant complexities that have not yet been fully explored in the existing literature. In this study, we systematically revisit and rigorously reformulate the cross-correlation method in the frequency domain, explicitly addressing and resolving issues related to non-zero covariances induced by windowing and overlapping of data in the time domain. We provide new expressions for the narrowband estimators and their covariances, which differ from those used in past searches. Fortunately, we show that the expressions that have been widely used in the field nonetheless lead to correct posterior distributions for parameter estimation and correct log-Bayes factors for model selection. By establishing a robust theoretical framework, our work facilitates more accurate and physically insightful interpretations of stochastic gravitational-wave background observations, laying an essential foundation for current and future research in this field.

</details>


### [96] [Primordial Black Holes: A Review of Formation and Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23846)

Method: 系统梳理PBH形成的流体动力学复杂性，建立相对论性坍缩阈值，分析原初等离子体中的非线性声速竞争，运用压缩函数的严格数学框架；同时纳入动态FLRW背景、高曲率修正以及记忆负担效应导致的量子反作用，重新审视霍金蒸发过程。

Result: 极端曲率环境会完全终止霍金蒸发，留下普朗克尺度残骸，这些残骸可规避当前河外星系观测限；下一代引力波观测站有望探测到亚太阳质量并合事件，为PBH范式提供确凿证据。

Conclusion: PBH不仅能作为暗物质候选者，更可作为检验高能物理的独特实验室，多信使观测将推动这一范式转变。

Abstract: Primordial Black Holes (PBHs) have emerged as a leading non-particulate candidate for dark matter and a unique cosmological probe, a paradigm shift accelerated by the detection of anomalous binary mergers by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration. While the literature is rich with phenomenological constraints, the fundamental quantum and relativistic underpinnings governing PBH genesis and evolution often receive comparatively less emphasis. This review aims to bridge that gap by systematically detailing the physics of PBH formation and their subsequent evolutionary trajectory. We critically examine the hydrodynamic complexity of the early universe, establishing the relativistic thresholds for collapse, the non-linear race against sound in the primordial plasma, and the rigorous mathematical utility of the compaction function. Furthermore, by incorporating the dynamic nature of FLRW backgrounds, higher curvature corrections, and quantum backreaction via the memory burden effect, we challenge the standard hawking evaporation and show that extreme-curvature environments halt evaporation entirely, leaving Planck-scale relics that evade current extragalactic bounds. Finally, we map the multimessenger observational landscape, highlighting how the imminent search for sub-solar mass inspirals by next-generation gravitational wave observatories -- such as the Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer -- could yield smoking-gun evidence for the PBH paradigm, ultimately transforming these primordial relics into unparalleled laboratories for high-energy physics.

### [97] [Energy Extraction via Magnetic Reconnection from a Rotating Dyonic Black Hole in $N = 2, \ U(1)^2$ Gauged Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23862)
*Raid M Suleiman,Shanshan Rodriguez,Dominic O. Chang,Leo Rodriguez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维N=2, U(1)²规范超引力中旋转带洞黑洞通过磁重联提取能量的机制。利用Comisso-Asenjo机制在ZAMO系中推导渐近流体能量，发现磁化截止参数和能量提取效率受规范耦合常数和带洞电荷的严格控制，且提取功率和效率随自旋非单调变化，在中等自旋(a~0.8)时达到峰值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旋转带洞黑洞通过磁重联提取能量的物理机制，探索规范耦合、带洞电荷、NUT参数等对Comisso-Asenjo能量提取过程的影响，特别关注与Kerr黑洞的差异。

Method: 在ZAMO参考系中应用Comisso-Asenjo机制，通过变分自旋a、电/磁电荷、NUT参数N_g和规范耦合g，计算截止磁化参数σ₀^cutoff，映射满足ε^∞_-<0的参数空间区域。

Result: σ₀^cutoff和CA能量提取的存在性受g和带洞电荷严格控制；增大g或使电荷趋近极端值会提高σ₀^cutoff并缩小CA活跃的能层区域。提取功率和效率在自旋a~0.8时达到峰值，无需近极端旋转；高效率需要极端磁化和近乎径向的外流。

Conclusion: 与Kerr黑洞不同，自旋通过归一化因子Ξ和四次地平函数Δ_g影响能量提取，AdS/NUT几何效应主导了通常的参考系拖曳增强。活跃的重联层被限制在视界外薄壳区域内。

Abstract: We study energy extraction via magnetic reconnection from a rotating dyonic black hole in four-dimensional $N=2$, $U(1)^2$ gauged supergravity. Using the Comisso-Asenjo mechanism in the ZAMO frame, we derive the asymptotic hydrodynamic energy per unit enthalpy $ε^{\infty}_\pm$ and determine when reconnection outflows attained negative energy at infinity. By varying the spin $a$, electric and magnetic charges, NUT parameter $N_g$, and gauge coupling $g$, we compute the cutoff magnetization $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and map the region of parameter space that admits $ε^{\infty}_-<0$. We find that $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and the very existence of Comisso-Asenjo extraction are tightly controlled by $g$ and the dyonic charges: increasing $g$ or pushing the charges toward extremality raises $σ_0^{\rm cutoff}$ and shrinks the CA-active part of the ergoregion. Unlike Kerr, the spin enters through the normalization factor $Ξ$, and the quartic horizon function $Δ_g$, so geometric effects from the AdS/NUT deformation dominate the usual frame-dragging enhancement. As a result, the extracted power and efficiency are non-monotonic in $a$ and peak at intermediate spin ($a\sim0.8$); near-extremal rotation is not required for high efficiency, provided $g$ is small and $Q$ is moderate. Efficient extraction further demands extreme magnetization and nearly radial outflows, confining the active reconnection layer to a thin shell, just outside the horizon.

### [98] [Newtonian Shirokov Effect: Epicyclic Frequency Splitting from Mass Multipoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23912)
*Anuar Idrissov,Kuantay Boshkayev,Abylaikhan Tlemissov,Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析了轴对称牛顿势中近圆轨道的小振动，作为相对论Shirokov效应的经典对应。通过计算等效势的完整Hessian矩阵并精确求解耦合双模振子，发现：四极矩分裂径向和垂直本征频率（等价于经典拱点与节点进动差），偶极矩不产生分裂（可被质心重新定义消除），八极矩确实产生分裂。频率分裂测量扁率J₂，轨道倾角测量质心偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究牛顿引力中轴对称势下近圆轨道的小振动，建立相对论Shirokov效应的经典对应，并系统分析各多极矩对轨道频率分裂的影响及其可观测性。

Method: 计算有效势在真实（可能倾斜）平衡点处的完整Hessian矩阵，精确求解耦合的双模振子系统。

Result: 四极矩导致Ω_θ²-Ω_r²=-3GQ/r₀⁵=6GMJ₂R²/r₀⁵的一阶分裂；偶极矩不产生频率分裂（可被质心重定义吸收）；八极矩产生ω₊²-ω₋²≈6G|O|/r₀⁶的分裂。轨道倾角δθ₀≃-r_CM/r₀可测量质心偏移。

Conclusion: 除偶极矩外所有多极矩都导致频率分裂，频率分裂测量扁率J₂，轨道倾角测量质心偏移。四极效应导致的横向漂移在1 au处约10⁻⁸ cm，与Shirokov的Schwarzschild估计相当。

Abstract: We analyze small oscillations of nearly circular orbits in an axisymmetric Newtonian potential expanded in mass multipoles, as the classical counterpart of the relativistic Shirokov effect. Computing the full Hessian of the effective potential at the true (possibly tilted) equilibrium and solving the coupled two-mode oscillator exactly, we obtain a complete picture. (i) A quadrupole splits the radial and vertical epicyclic frequencies, $Ω_θ^2-Ω_r^2=-3GQ/r_0^5=6GMJ_2R^2/r_0^5$, at first order in $J_2$; the Newtonian analogue of the Shirokov splitting, equivalent to the classical statement that an oblate body's apsidal and nodal rates differ. (ii) A gravitational dipole produces no splitting: it equals $M r_{\rm CM}$, is removable by re-centering at the center of mass, and cannot appear in any coordinate-independent frequency; the apparent first-order coupling cancels at the true tilted equilibrium, any residual absorbed by the induced quadrupole of the shifted source, confirmed by direct orbit integration. (iii) A genuine octupole does split the frequencies, $ω_+^2-ω_-^2\approx6G|O|/r_0^6$. The selection rule is thus not even/odd parity: every multipole splits the frequencies except the dipole. These yield two complementary probes of an axisymmetric source: the frequency splitting measures the oblateness $J_2$, while the orbital-plane tilt, $δθ_0\simeq-r_{\rm CM}/r_0$, measures the center-of-mass offset $r_{\rm CM}$, an orbital-geometry observable rather than a frequency one. We give solar-system estimates for both. Carried through to Shirokov's original observable -- the secular transverse drift after $n$ orbits -- the quadrupole effect gives $ξ^θ=ξ_0^θ\,πn\,(6J_2R^2/r_0^2)$, of order $10^{-8}$ cm at $1$ au and $\sim10^{-6}$ cm near $0.1$ au, comparable to Shirokov's Schwarzschild estimate.

</details>


### [99] [Nonrotating and rotating black holes with secondary disformal hair in a ghost-free metric-affine parity-violating scalar-torsion theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24041)
*E. Brito,G. Macedo,J. R. Nascimento,A. Yu. Petrov,P. J. Porfírio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个无鬼影的度规-仿射标量-挠率模型，其中赝标量场与Nieh-Yan密度耦合，并与Einstein-Palatini张量导数耦合。在射影不变性和平移对称性下，独立联络被精确求解：其对称部分是与度规h_{μν}（与g_{μν}非共形相关）关联的Levi-Civita联络，反对称部分是纯轴矢量挠率。在分支α=6β²κ²下，h-度规框架中的Ricci平坦几何可解度规方程且Noether流恒为零。以Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞为例，在h-框架中构造了标量场轮廓，并讨论了g-框架中由非平凡标量场产生的非共形修正和二级标量毛发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构造一个在射影变换下不变、无鬼影的度规-仿射标量-挠率引力理论，并研究其黑洞解和标量毛发特性。

Method: 引入赝标量场与Nieh-Yan密度耦合及与Einstein-Palatini张量的导数耦合；在射影规范固定后精确求解独立联络；识别无鬼影退化分支并求解场方程。

Result: 在退化分支下，h-度规框架中的Ricci平坦几何（如Schwarzschild和Kerr）解度规方程；构造了静态和含时标量场轮廓；在g-框架中得到了非共形变形和二级标量毛发。

Conclusion: 该理论中存在无鬼影分支，黑洞解在h-框架中为隐身解，在g-框架中表现为具有非平凡标量场轮廓的二级非共形毛发，而非初级Noether荷毛发。

Abstract: In this paper, we formulate a ghost-free metric-affine scalar-torsion model in which a pseudoscalar field is coupled to the Nieh--Yan density and derivatively coupled to the Einstein-Palatini tensor. The theory is projectively invariant and, in the shift-symmetric sector, depends on the scalar only through its gradient. After fixing the projective gauge, the independent connection is solved exactly: its symmetric part is the Levi-Civita connection associated with the metric \(h_{μν}\), disformally related to the metric $g_{μν}$, while its antisymmetric part is a purely axial torsion sourced by $v_μ=\partial_μ\vartheta$. We identify a degenerate ghost-free branch, $α=6β^2κ^2$, for which Ricci-flat geometries in the $h$-metric frame solve the metric equations and the Noether current vanishes identically. For example, we consider Schwarzschild and Kerr geometries in the $h$-metric frame, which generate disformal deformations on these geometries from the perspective of the $g$-metric frame. For the Schwarzschild black hole in the $h$-metric frame, we construct static and Babichev--Charmousis-like time-dependent scalar profiles, and discuss horizon regularity in Eddington--Finkelstein coordinates. For the Kerr black hole in the $h$-metric frame, we show that the fixed-norm scalar profile is generically axisymmetric, depending on both the radial and angular coordinates, and we construct a stationary future-regular profile in ingoing Kerr coordinates. The Kerr solution with the nontrivial scalar field is stealth only in the $h$-metric frame. In the $g$-metric frame, it produces disformal corrections stemming from the nontrivial scalar field profile and it represents secondary disformal scalar hair rather than primary Noether-charge hair.

### [100] [Nanohertz gravitational waves from domain walls nucleated during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24070)
*Zhi-Yong Huang,Tie-Jun Gao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了暴胀期间通过量子隧穿产生的畴壁所引发的标量诱导引力波。与瞬时成核框架不同，有限成核持续时间导致畴壁半径分布参数γ>1，增强了曲率扰动，使SIGW峰值可达纳赫兹频段且振幅可被探测。通过构建双场暴胀模型，计算了匹配NANOGrav和EPTA信号的SIGW谱，并预测了其他引力波探测器可能观测到的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建包含暴胀子φ和 spectator场χ的双场暴胀模型，通过势能V(φ,χ)耦合，使得畴壁张力σ(t)在暴胀子滚动经过临界值时平滑演化。该转变的特征宽度决定了曲率功率谱的截断尺度k_cut，从而将SIGW峰值置于纳赫兹频段。

Result: 对于三个代表性参数集，计算得到的SIGW谱与NANOGrav和EPTA的纳赫兹信号匹配。通过选择不同参数，模型还可同时预测其他引力波探测器可能观测到的信号。

Conclusion: 有限成核持续时间通过半径分布增强曲率扰动，使畴壁诱导的引力波信号足以解释当前脉冲星计时阵列观测，并为未来多频段引力波探测提供可检验预测。

Abstract: We investigate scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) produced by domain walls (DWs) nucleated via quantum tunneling during inflation with an extended nucleation time. In contrast to the small-period nucleation framework, where DWs form instantaneously and produce a curvature power spectrum too weak to account for the nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) reported by pulsar timing array (PTA) collaborations, we show that a finite nucleation duration leads to a distribution of DW radii characterized by $γ\equiv\overline{R^4}/(\overline{R^2})^2>1$, which enhances the resulting curvature perturbations. We construct a two-field inflation model with an inflaton $φ$ and a spectator field $χ$ coupled through the potential $V(φ,χ)$, where the DW tension $σ(t)$ evolves smoothly as the inflaton rolls past a critical value. The characteristic width of this transition determines the cutoff scale $k_{\text{cut}}$ of the curvature power spectrum, enabling the SIGW peak to be placed in the nanohertz frequency band with detectable amplitude. For three representative parameter sets, we compute the SIGW spectra and find that the nanohertz-peaked spectrum matching the NANOGrav and EPTA signals. By selecting different parameters, our model simultaneously predicts potentially observable signals at other gravitational-wave detectors.

### [101] [Nonlinear Stability of Kerr-Sen Black Holes in Merging Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24215)
*Andrew Carroll,Eric W. Hirschmann,Hyun Lim,David Neilsen,David F. Van Komen,Sebastian Vander Ploeg Fallon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟，研究了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-膨胀子-轴子理论中的Kerr-Sen黑洞稳定性，发现带电黑洞在并合后膨胀场持续存在，自旋黑洞则保留轴子场，且初始非标量化的Kerr-Newman黑洞在标量背景下会获得并保持标量化，这些结果表明该黑洞在该替代引力理论中是稳定的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Kerr-Sen黑洞在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-膨胀子-轴子理论中的稳定性，探索这类替代引力理论中黑洞的动力学行为。

Method: 采用数值相对论框架，使用近似初始数据进行头对撞双黑洞数值模拟，覆盖部分参数空间。

Result: (1) 带电黑洞并合后膨胀场持续存在；(2) 自旋黑洞并合后保留轴子场；(3) 初始非标量化的黑洞在标量背景下会获得并保持标量毛发；(4) 初始非标量化的Kerr-Newman黑洞会标量化并保持。

Conclusion: 这些场在并合后长时间持续存在，强烈表明Kerr-Sen黑洞在该替代引力理论中是稳定的。

Abstract: We investigate the stability of Kerr-Sen black holes, which arise in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton-axion theory. Within a numerical relativity framework, we perform head-on binary black hole simulations with approximate initial data across a portion of the parameter space. We find that for nontrivial electric charge, a dilaton field persists through merger and that in the presence of spin, the remnant will also retain an axion field. The persistence of these fields for long times after merger strongly suggests the stability of these black holes within this alternative gravity theory. We further test whether initially unscalarized black holes will acquire hair in the presence of a scalar background. We find that black holes immersed in such a background retain scalar hair. Furthermore, we find that even initially unscalarized Kerr-Newman black holes will scalarize and remain scalarized throughout the evolution.

### [102] [Reduction of the Finsler gravity vacuum equation and dynamics for the cosmological Landsberg spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24698)
*Christian Pfeifer,Fidel F. Villaseñor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了标量Finsler引力真空方程简化为Finsler Ricci曲率为零的条件，发现当存在某个幂次F^n足够正则且其Finsler度量在光锥上非退化，同时Landsberg项为零时，可实现这种简化。该结果推广了以往要求F^2正则的强假设，并应用于求解Landsberg型均匀各向同性Finsler时空的引力方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Finsler引力（广义相对论在相空间视角下的推广）中，真空Einstein方程直接简化为Ricci张量为零，但Finsler引力中这种简化并不直接。本文旨在找出标量Finsler引力真空方程（纯度规或Palatini形式）简化为Finsler Ricci曲率为零的精确条件。

Method: 通过解析论证，分析Finsler函数F的幂次F^n的正则性及其相关Finsler度量在光锥上的非退化性，结合Landsberg项的消失条件，推导真空方程的简化条件。并将结果应用于Landsberg型均匀各向同性Finsler时空的求解。

Result: 发现当存在某个幂次F^n足够正则且其Finsler度量在光锥上非退化，同时Landsberg项为零时，标量Finsler引力真空方程可简化为Finsler Ricci曲率为零。该结果推广了[Villasenor2024]中要求F^2正则的较强假设。

Conclusion: 本文建立的简化条件显著推广了已有结果，使得更多Finsler引力模型（不满足F^2正则的模型）的真空方程求解更加可行，并在Landsberg型均匀各向同性时空中展示了其应用价值。

Abstract: When solving the Einstein vacuum equations, a very helpful feature is that they reduce simply to the vanishing of the Ricci tensor. In Finsler gravity, a promising extension of general relativity that can describe the gravitational field of kinetic gases from a phase space perspective in terms of Finsler geometry, such a reduction is not as straightforward.
  In this article, we identify precise conditions under which the scalar Finsler gravity vacuum equation (in either its purely metric or its Palatini formulation) reduces to the vanishing of the Finslerian Ricci curvature. Through analytic arguments, we find that this happens if there exists some power $F^n$ of the Finsler function $F$ that is sufficiently regular and whose associated Finsler metric is non-degenerate on the light cones. Moreover, the Landsberg term in the scalar equation must vanish. This result significantly generalizes the findings of [Villasenor2024], where a reduction theorem was established under the quite strong assumption that $F^2$ is regular, which is not satisfied by many examples currently under consideration.
  We demonstrate the impact of our findings by applying them to solve the Finsler gravity equations for homogeneous and isotropic Finsler spacetime functions of Landsberg type.

</details>

Method: 采用开放量子系统框架，将克尔黑洞周围的轴子云作为多模压缩引力环境；利用Takagi分解处理复对称压缩核，将引力子场分解为具有反常关联子的独立压缩超模；通过求迹引力子浴，结合弱相互作用诱导的味混合，推导对称与反对称两介子扇区之间的跃迁。

Result: 获得了ω参数的显式表达式，表现为Takagi超模的求和，权重为各超模的压缩幅度和相位以及弱相互作用味混合矩阵元；表明ω效应可能是一般性量子引力非经典态的通用特征，不限于轴子云场景。

Abstract: The $ω$-effect in entangled neutral-meson systems provides a sensitive probe of CPT violation induced by quantum-gravitational environments. In open quantum systems, interactions with inaccessible gravitational degrees of freedom can render the reduced meson dynamics non-unitary, causing the CPT operator to become ill-defined, even when the underlying microscopic Hamiltonian is CPT invariant. We present a microscopic derivation of the $ω$-effect arising from a multimode squeezed gravitational environment generated by an axion cloud around a Kerr black hole. Using the Takagi decomposition of the associated complex symmetric squeezing kernel, the graviton field is expressed in terms of independent squeezed supermodes possessing anomalous correlators. These correlators provide a microscopic quantum counterpart of the stochastic fluctuations that appear in earlier D-particle foam descriptions of the $ω$-effect, replacing phenomenological variances of flavour-changing D-particle recoil by calculable graviton correlation functions. After tracing over the graviton bath, the anomalous correlators and the weak-interactions-induced mixing combine to generate transitions between the antisymmetric and symmetric two-meson sectors. This results in a small exchange-symmetric admixture, parametrised by $ω$, in the otherwise antisymmetric EPR state. We obtain an explicit expression for $ω$ in terms of a sum over Takagi supermodes weighted by their squeezing amplitudes and phases together with the weak-interaction flavour-mixing matrix element. The resulting framework suggests that the $ω$-effect may be a generic signature of non-classical states of gravitational environments, extending beyond the specific axion-cloud scenario considered here. The observability of the $ω$-effect from other astrophysical and microscopic black-hole sources is discussed.

### [107] [When Black Holes Can Wear Pants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24642)
*Giacomo Cacciapaglia,Manuel Del Piano,Francesco Sannino,Vania Vellucci*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞视界分裂（即"裤子拓扑"）是否可能在物理上实现，澄清其发生的理论条件，这对于理解原初黑洞演化及黑洞并合等灾难性事件具有重要意义。

Method: 首先在经典广义相对论框架下分析Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞的熵与运动学约束；随后考察多种可能促成分裂的场景：高维Gregory-Laflamme不稳定性、非轴对称辐射 trapping中的超辐射不稳定性、以及四维修改引力模型中熵/视界半径与质量关系的变更。

Result: Schwarzschild黑洞被Bekenstein-Hawking面积律严格禁止分裂；Kerr黑洞在纯运动学分析下也存在约束，仅在近极端情形可能例外。高维和修改引力模型中熵可能支持小碎片发射，但分裂是否发生仍取决于初始态的运动学构型。

Conclusion: 黑洞分裂在多数经典场景中受到严格抑制，熵有利并不保证动力学可行，运动学约束是关键限制因素。该结论对原初黑洞和黑洞并合事件有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the conditions under which black hole fragmentation, the splitting of a black hole horizon into multiple smaller ones, may occur. The simplest realization is that of a single black hole horizon splitting into two, giving rise to the eponymous pants topology. In classical general relativity, the Bekenstein-Hawking area law forbids such processes for Schwarzschild black holes. For spinning Kerr black holes, purely kinematic analyses impose constraints that prevent fragmentation, even in regimes where entropy considerations might allow it, except possibly in near-extremal cases. We then hunt for scenarios where black holes can wear pants: from the well-known Gregory-Laflamme instability in higher dimensions, to the potential effect of superradiant instabilities in non-axisymmetric radiation trapping, to finally gravitational models that modify the relations between entropy and/or horizon radius and the black hole mass in four dimensions. In all such cases, emission of small fragments can be entropically favored, however its occurrence still depends on the kinematic configuration of the initial state. Our analysis clarifies the theoretical landscape where black holes may fragment, which is particularly relevant for primordial black holes and catastrophic events such as black hole mergers.

Abstract: We revisit the convergence region of the quasinormal modes expansion of Schwarzschild retarded Green functions from a radial scattering viewpoint. The tortoise coordinate admits a natural reflection about a distinguished point, which maps the original Regge-Wheeler problem to a mirror radial problem with the same quasinormal mode spectrum. Although this reflection is not a spacetime symmetry and does not leave the potential invariant, it gives a simple image interpretation of the second lightcone distance that controls convergence. Equivalently, after folding the radial line at the reflection point, the direct and mirror contributions arise as diagonal and off-diagonal propagation channels of a two-component half-line problem. We also relate this structure to the AdS$_2$ Green function, where the same direct-plus-image lightcone structure arises from a genuine boundary-bouncing null geodesic. This provides a spectral interpretation of the convergence condition and clarifies the role of the reflection point in the Schwarzschild radial Green function.

Abstract: As LISA and other next-generation detectors demand increasingly accurate waveform models, there is a growing need for these models to precisely control gauge freedoms that had previously been inconsequential. One such intrinsic freedom is the choice of the asymptotic Bondi--Metzner--Sachs (BMS) frame. The need to control the BMS frame is particularly pronounced in black hole perturbation theory, where there has been little work to this end -- most glaringly in gravitational self-force calculations, which are in an unknown frame and encounter infrared, far-zone gauge singularities at second perturbative order. Here we present a framework for iteratively transforming to the Bondi--Sachs gauge and fixing the BMS frame on a Kerr background. This includes an extension of the Bondi--Sachs formalism to the multiscale expansions that underpin most self-force-based waveforms, introducing soft hair and a concept of ``forgetful gauges'' in the process. Our framework evades infrared divergences and naturally incorporates memory effects that had previously only ever been added ``after the fact'' in self-force waveforms, including the recently discovered ``memory distortion''. Our formalism could also be used for ringdown analysis, and we expect it to be vital for comparisons with numerical relativity and post-Newtonian theory.

We then analyze the algebraic conditions that permit Lifshitz backgrounds, both in the absence and in the presence of the massive vector field. Since closed-form black-hole solutions are not available for the generic quintic theory, we construct numerical solutions using near-horizon expansions and a shooting method. We present solutions for the relativistic branch \(z=1\) and the Lifshitz branch \(z=2\), covering the three horizon topologies \(k=-1,0,+1\). The numerical profiles of the metric functions and the gauge-field function show behavior that is qualitatively consistent with earlier studies of cubic and quartic quasi-topological Lifshitz black holes.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论的背景独立性要求为量子几何和物质场选择合适的希尔伯特空间表示提供了物理选择，但现有非微扰正则量子化方案的希尔伯特空间不可分，导致量子化歧义。因此，需要一种背景独立且可分的表示来提高理论的可预测性。

Method: 作者构建了严格的、背景独立的Fock表示，用于几何和物质场的非微扰正则量子化。该表示的关键特点是其Fock希尔伯特空间是可分的，这与其它非微扰正则量子化方案（如圈量子引力）的不可分希尔伯特空间形成对比。

Result: 得到了一个可分的Fock希尔伯特空间表示，并以此为基础讨论了宇宙学截断和量子反弹机制。

Conclusion: 背景独立的Fock表示可能有助于得到显著更具预测性的量子引力理论，因为可分性减少了量子化歧义。

Abstract: A UV complete quantum field theory of general relativity is believed to require a non-perturbative approach. Moreover, background independence of classical general relativity supplies a physical selection for suitable Hilbert space representations of the quantum geometry and matter fields.
  In this contribution we show that, contrary to common intuition, there exist rigorous, background independent Fock representations available for a non-perturbative canonical quantisation of geometry and suitable matter fields.
  This is interesting because the Fock Hilbert space is separable while the Hilbert space of other manifestly background independent and non-perturbative canonical quantisation programmes is not. Since non-separability is a source for quantisation ambiguities, such a Fock representation may help to arrive at a significantly more predictive theory. As a simple application we discuss the cosmological truncation and mechanisms for quantum bounces.
  To make this manuscript concise we focus on the simplest incarnation of this idea. More details and many extensions are supplied in a companion paper.

</details>


### [112] [Fermionic Love number of higher-dimensional Reissner-Nordström black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24365)
*Xiankai Pang,Yu Tian,Hongbao Zhang,Qingquan Jiang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将费米子潮汐Love数推广到高维Reissner-Nordström黑洞，发现费米子TLNs在所有维度$D \geq 4$和角动量$l$下均非零（除极端黑洞外），且随维度增加$l$依赖性减弱，在无限维极限下完全消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前关于费米子潮汐Love数(TLNs)的工作推广至更高维度的Reissner-Nordström黑洞，探索维度对费米子TLNs的影响。

Method: 在$D$维时空中使用内入爱丁顿坐标和正则标架求解无质量Dirac方程，识别正则解分支后，从无穷远处的渐近行为提取费米子TLNs。

Result: 费米子TLNs展现出丰富的维度依赖结构；与玻色子TLNs在$D>4$时对某些$l$消失不同，费米子TLNs对所有$l$和$D \geq 4$均非零（极端黑洞除外）；$l$依赖性随$D$增加而减弱，在无限维极限下完全消失。

Conclusion: 为高维时空中黑洞对费米子扰动的响应提供了新见解。

Abstract: In this paper, we generalize our previous work on the fermionic tidal Love numbers (TLNs) to higher-dimensional Reissner-Nordström black holes. The massless Dirac equation is solved in $D$-dimensional spacetime using ingoing Eddington coordinates and regular tetrads. After identifying the regular solution branch, we extract the fermionic TLNs from its asymptotic behavior at infinity. The resulting TLNs exhibit a rich dimension-dependent structure that generalizes the four-dimensional case. Unlike bosonic TLNs, which vanish for certain values of the total angular momentum $l$ in dimensions $D>4$, fermionic TLNs remain non-zero for all $l$ and $D \geq 4$, except for extremal black holes. Moreover, the $l$-dependence weakens as $D$ increases, disappearing entirely in the infinite-dimensional limit. These results provide new insights into black hole responses to fermionic perturbations in higher-dimensional spacetimes.

### [113] [Spectroscopy and Dissociation of Tetraquarks in Anisotropic Plasma within the Generalized Fractional Derivatives Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23732)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究奇异多夸克态的光谱学和热稳定性对于理解极端条件下量子色动力学（QCD）的基本禁闭机制至关重要。

Method: 采用广义分数阶导数（GFD）结构，利用包含德拜屏蔽和各向异性效应的扩展Cornell势，通过参数化广义分数阶Nikiforov-Uvarov（PGFNU）技术求解径向薛定谔方程。

Result: 束缚势和解离能随各向异性参数增大而增大，随温度升高而减小；分数阶越低，系统束缚越强；计算了cc\bar{c}\bar{c}、bb\bar{b}\bar{b}、c\bar{q}c\bar{q}、b\bar{q}b\bar{q}的基态和激发态质量谱。

Abstract: Investigating the spectroscopy and thermal stability of exotic multiquark states provides crucial insights into the fundamental confinement mechanisms of quantum chromodynamics (QCD) under extreme regimes. This work presents an innovative study of the spectroscopy and dissociation of fully-heavy tetraquarks in an anisotropic plasma via the generalized fractional derivative (GFD) structure. The radial Schrödinger equation (SE) with an extended Cornell potential that includes Debye screening and plasma anisotropy into account is solved by applying the parametric generalised fractional Nikiforov-Uvarov (PGFNU) technique. The analysis of systems consisting of $cc\bar c\bar c$ and $bb\bar{b}\bar{b}$ shows that the binding potential of the systems and the dissociation energy increase with the anisotropy parameter and decrease with temperature. The fractional paradigm also shows that when the fractional orders are lower, the systems will be more strongly bound than in classical quantum mechanics. Furthermore, the mass spectra for all considered tetraquark configurations, including the $cc\bar{c}\bar{c}$, $bb\bar{b}\bar{b}$, $c\bar{q}c\bar{q}$, and $b\bar{q}b\bar{q}$ systems, are calculated for both ground and excited states. These calculations were performed across both the fractional and classical regimes. The findings indicate that the GFD framework provides an effective mathematical basis for modelling hadronic systems in complex contexts, and they demonstrate significant agreement with earlier theoretical studies.

### [114] [From Magnetic to Inverse Magnetic Catalysis: The Interplay of Quark and Gluon Mass Generation in Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23736)

Result: 磁场增强夸克质量导致磁催化，同时增强胶子屏蔽质量；后者在相变点附近占主导，产生逆磁催化。

Conclusion: 胶子屏蔽质量的增强构成了与磁催化竞争的机制，并在手征相变附近主导了逆磁催化现象。

Abstract: We analyze the effects of the magnetic field on the quark and gluon propagators within the functional QCD framework. By solving the coupled Dyson-Schwinger equations for the quark and gluon propagators, we find that the quark mass is generally enhanced in the presence of a magnetic field, leading to magnetic catalysis of the chiral condensate. Meanwhile, the magnetic field also induces an increase in the gluon screening mass. The enhancement of the gluon screening mass suppresses the quark-gluon interaction and thereby weakens the strength of dynamical chiral symmetry breaking, establishing a competing mechanism against magnetic catalysis. In particular, this enhancement of the gluon screening mass becomes dominant near the chiral phase transition, which in turn gives rise to inverse magnetic catalysis.

Abstract: While QCD fundamentally only depends on the values of the strong coupling and the quark masses, it exhibits a rich nonperturbative structure at low energies, where composite fields emerge as the relevant degrees of freedom. In this work, we present a first-principles framework that captures the transition from fundamental QCD to its low-energy sector in vacuum. It builds on the dynamical hadronization technique within the functional renormalization group approach to two-flavor QCD. In this framework, the low-energy constants relevant for effective models, including effective masses and coupling strengths, naturally emerge from the underlying renormalization group flow without introducing free parameters beyond those of QCD itself. We investigate the dynamical emergence of the pion, the $σ$-meson and the scalar diquark in both imaginary and real time, and determine a set of QCD low-energy constants which can be used to fix the free parameters of models of dense quark matter with a two-flavor color superconducting phase. In particular, this includes previously unknown properties of the scalar diquark. Our results provide important microscopic input for constraining color superconducting phases, which are expected to play a key role in our understanding of dense neutron star matter.

The presence of an ultra-light PBH dominated epoch not only ensures sufficient production of RHNs, but also keeps the leptogenesis scenario free from strong washout problem of thermal leptogenesis at very high scale. In addition, the PBH dominated epoch also helps in generating a gravitational bremsstrahlung spectrum distinct from the stochastic GW background from the thermal bath. Finally, PBH evaporation also brings two separate sources of GW via density perturbation and graviton emission via Hawking evaporation. For the most optimistic scenario with very high scale seesaw consistent with neutrino mass and leptogenesis, this leads to a multi-peaked GW spectrum with peak frequencies lying in the MHz-EHz range.

Result: 获得了替代方案下的NLO劈裂函数和反常维度，发现主导行为可自然地解释为修正的有效演化标度。

Conclusion: 这是朝着能够在替代方案中演化和拟合PDF以用于QCD计算迈出的关键一步。

Abstract: Beyond leading order, parton distribution functions (PDFs) require a choice of factorisation scheme to be defined unambiguously. Different choices of factorisation scheme lead to PDFs that satisfy modified DGLAP evolution equations, relative to the conventional $\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$ scheme. In this paper we derive the NLO DGLAP splitting functions for PDFs in alternative factorisation schemes, including for a parametrised scheme spanning a subspace of the general factorisation-scheme space. We plot their Mellin-space counterparts, the anomalous dimensions, and study the leading large- and small-$x$ behaviour, relevant to resummation. We find that the leading behaviour admits a natural interpretation as a modified effective evolution scale. This is an essential step towards being able to evolve and fit PDFs in alternative schemes for use within QCD calculations.

</details>


### [122] [Polarized Deep-Inelastic Scattering with Spin Correlations in Herwig 7](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23845)

TL;DR: 本文在Herwig 7中实现了极化深度非弹性散射的NLO+POWHEG匹配，构建了自旋关联处理方案，并验证了初态自旋密度初始化对部分观测量有显著影响，而实发射自旋信息在纵向极化情形下影响不显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的背景下，需要为极化深度非弹性散射（DIS）提供完整的、满足NLO精度的蒙特卡洛模拟工具，以正确描述自旋依赖的强相互作用过程。

Conclusion: 所构建的自旋关联处理方案有效且自洽，其中初态自旋信息对部分观测量具有实际影响，而实发射自旋信息的额外贡献在纵向极化情形下可忽略，为EIC的极化物理模拟提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: We investigate polarized deep-inelastic scattering (DIS) in the context of fully exclusive Monte Carlo simulations for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). We present a next-to-leading-order (NLO) treatment of polarized DIS in Herwig 7 using the POWHEG matching scheme, including neutral-current $γ/Z$ exchange and charged-current scattering. We also construct a spin-correlation treatment for NLO-matched events, first by initializing the shower from the spin-density matrix of the polarized DIS Born process and then by propagating the spin-density matrix of the accepted real-emission configuration without changing the POWHEG event weight or hardest-emission choice. We validate the integrated cross sections against fixed-order calculations, use parton-level comparisons without subsequent shower evolution to isolate the accepted POWHEG real-emission kinematics, and employ shower-level observables to test the numerical importance of the Born-level and real-emission spin information. We find that the Born-level spin-density initialization can have a visible impact on shower-sensitive observables, while the additional spin information from the accepted real-emission configuration is not resolved for the longitudinally polarized observables considered here.

### [123] [Event isotropy in perturbative QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23924)
*Daniele Atzori,Matteo Cacciari,Simone Marzani,Gregory Soyez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在微扰QCD框架下系统研究了碰撞事件的各向同性观测量（Event Isotropy），基于能量移动距离（EMD）定义，在$e^+e^-$对撞中实现了$O(α_s)$半解析计算、$O(α_s^2)$（NLO）数值计算，并完成了NLL精度下的全阶求和与NLL+NLO匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来EMD的提出使得对撞事件可被赋予度量结构，从而用几何语言重新描述对撞物理并定义新观测量。事件各向同性（Event Isotropy）作为其中之一，尚缺乏微扰QCD框架下的理论计算，因此需要建立其微扰预言以推动该观测量在实际对撞分析中的应用。

Method: 在$e^+e^-$碰撞中：1) 在$O(α_s)$（领头阶）下进行半解析计算；2) 在$O(α_s^2)$（次领头阶）下进行数值计算；3) 通过重求和软共线发射贡献，达到NLL精度；4) 将重求和结果与固定阶结果匹配，实现NLL+NLO精度。

Result: 实现了事件各向同性在$e^+e^-$碰撞中从领头阶到NLL+NLO精度的理论预言，包括$O(α_s)$半解析结果、$O(α_s^2)$数值结果以及NLL精度的全阶重求和结果。

Conclusion: 通过匹配重求和与固定阶计算，得到了NLL+NLO精度的事件各向同性分布，为基于EMD的几何观测量提供了可靠的微扰QCD理论基础，有助于未来将其应用于对撞机物理分析。

Abstract: It has recently been proposed that collider events can be equipped with a metric, the Energy Mover's Distance (EMD), which allows one to rephrase multiple aspects of collider physics in a geometric language. Further, the EMD can be exploited to define new observables. In this context, event isotropy quantifies the resemblance of an event to a uniform energy distribution. We present the first theoretical study of event isotropy within the framework of perturbative QCD. In particular, we first obtain the isotropy distribution in $e^+e^-$ collisions semi-analytically at $O(α_s)$ (leading-order) and numerically at $O(α_s^2)$ (next-to-leading order, NLO). Furthermore, we obtain all-order theoretical predictions by resumming the contributions of soft and collinear emissions, at next-to-leading logarithmic (NLL) accuracy. By matching resummed and fixed-order predictions we reach NLL+NLO accuracy.

### [124] [Mapping jet substructure in heavy-ion collisions with track functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23971)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用JEWEL和HYBRID两种蒙特卡洛喷注淬火模型，计算径迹函数的各阶矩与累积量，分析其在真空与介质环境下的差异，并研究领头阶矩的重整化群流。

Result: 两种模型下径迹函数的高阶矩和累积量均显著偏离真空基线，但定量修正幅度差异明显；介质中领头阶矩的RG流与真空演化定性一致。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of high-energy QCD cascades in heavy-ion collisions, focusing on modifications to jets' substructure induced by the presence of a quark-gluon plasma (QGP). To this end, we study the properties and scale evolution of track functions, non-perturbative objects encoding the flow of energy from an initiating parton to all charged hadrons. In contrast to the more standard fragmentation functions, these objects have a non-linear renormalization group (RG) evolution, being sensitive to the entire jet fragmentation process. Using the JEWEL and HYBRID Monte-Carlo models of jet quenching, we find that in both frameworks the higher moments and cumulants of the track functions' distributions exhibit sizable deviations from their vacuum baselines, demonstrating that medium-induced energy loss imprints itself in the in-medium jet fragmentation pattern. We find that the quantitative magnitude of these modifications differs significantly between the two models. This identifies track functions as a class of observables capable of discriminating between competing microscopic pictures of jet-medium interactions. We further examined the (in-medium) RG flows for the leading moments, which remain in qualitative agreement with the in-vacuum evolution. This provides an avenue to directly test the RG flows inside a QGP, linking heavy-ion jet measurements to basic QFT understanding of partonic branching. Finally, we comment on the feasibility and challenges associated with extracting track functions from experimental data.

Abstract: As the lightest strange scalar resonance, $K_0^*(700)$ (also called $κ$) has a large width and resides close to the $Kπ$ threshold, leading to a longstanding debate about its internal structure. ### [127] [Non-holomorphic $S^{\prime}_{4}$ modular symmetry for leptons and leptogenesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24277)
*Cai-Chang Li,Jun-Nan Lu,Xiang-Yan Gao,Ming-Hua Weng,Gui-Jun Ding*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于非全纯S'_4模对称性，利用从-4到6整数权的4级多调和Maaß形式，系统研究了轻子模型。通过I型跷跷板机制和两个右手中微子产生轻中微子质量，仅引入模τ作为通量场，不施加广义CP对称性。数值分析得到36个可行模型（中微子质量正态序），每个模型仅含4个实耦合参数和模τ。这些模型分为三类，每类12个，对轻子可观测量的预测相似，主要区别在于E^c_1的分配。对每类代表模型的详细分析显示，它们对中微子质量和混合参数有非常清晰的预测，主要通过θ_23、δ_CP和α_21区分。只有两类代表模型能在无味区成功实现热轻子生成，用相同的参数值再现观测到的重子不对称性。在这些模型中，模τ的实部是轻子混合和轻子生成中CP破坏的唯一来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轻子模型研究多基于全纯模对称性，而非全纯模对称性（尤其是S'_4）的研究还不充分。本文旨在系统探索非全纯S'_4模对称性下轻子模型的可行性，通过使用更广泛的Maaß形式（多种权重）来构建模型，期望在无需额外通量场和广义CP对称性的条件下，以最少参数解释中微子质量和混合，并探索CP破坏来源和轻子生成机制。

Result: 发现36个可行模型（中微子质量正态序），每个模型仅含4个实耦合参数和模τ。模型分为三类，每类12个。代表模型对中微子质量和混合参数有非常清晰的预测，主要通过θ_23、δ_CP和α_21区分。其中两类代表模型成功实现热轻子生成，用相同参数值再现观测到的重子不对称性。模τ的实部是CP破坏的唯一来源。

Conclusion: 非全纯S'_4模对称性提供了一个简洁的框架，能以最少参数（仅4个实耦合和模τ）构建可行的轻子模型，解释中微子质量和混合，同时通过模τ实部统一解释轻子混合和轻子生成中的CP破坏。三类模型在θ_23、δ_CP和α_21上给出可区分的预言，为未来实验检验提供了明确方向。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive and systematic investigation of lepton models based on the non-holomorphic $S^{\prime}_{4}$ modular symmetry, by using level 4 polyharmonic Maaß forms spanning integer weights from $-4$ to $6$. The light neutrino masses are generated by the type-I seesaw mechanism with two right-handed neutrinos, no flavon fields other than the modulus $τ$ is introduced, and the generalized CP symmetry is not imposed. An exhaustive numerical analysis yields 36 viable models with only four real couplings besides the modulus $τ$ when neutrino masses are normal ordering. They are classified into three categories, each containing twelve models which yield quite similar predictions for lepton observables and are distinguished by the assignment of $E^c_1$. Furthermore, we perform a detailed numerical analysis for one representative model from each category. These representative models are found to yield very sharp predictions for neutrino masses and mixing parameters, and they are distinguished by the predictions for the atmospheric mixing angle $θ_{23}$, the Dirac CP phase $δ_{CP}$ and the Majorana CP phase $α_{21}$. Furthermore, we find that only two of these three representative models accommodate successful thermal leptogenesis in the unflavored regime, reproducing the observed baryon asymmetry with the identical parameter values that satisfy neutrino oscillation data. In these models, the real part of the modulus $τ$ is the unique source of CP violation in both lepton mixing and leptogenesis.

Abstract: Exotic hadrons beyond the conventional quark model provide a direct window into the dynamics of strong interaction. In this work, we introduce the neural-network quantum state (NNQS) approach to investigate the spectra of fully-heavy multiquark states within the non-relativistic potential quark model. By employing deep neural networks to represent the complex many-body spatial wave function, and constructing the color-spin part exactly from group theory to enforce fermionic antisymmetry, our approach effectively overcomes the dimensionality obstacles inherent in traditional methods. The results are compared with various model calculations, demonstrating that NNQS offers superior accuracy and flexibility, particularly in treating high-dimensional correlations. This work establishes NNQS as a promising tool for exploring the spectroscopy of exotic hadrons.

Conclusion: 高能μ子对撞机在测试b夸克电弱偶极相互作用方面具有显著优势，尤其通过μ⁺μ⁻→bb̅h过程可获得比现有手段更严格的约束。

Abstract: We study the sensitivity of a high-energy $μ-$collider with center of mass energy in the multi--TeV range in testing electroweak dipole interactions of the $b-$quark. We parametrize the relevant deformations in the language of the Standard Model effective field theory, where the dominant modifications arise at the $d=6$ level. We analyse $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b$ and $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b h$ scatterings, performing a study at the level of a fast detector simulation. Owing the chiral structure of the dipole interaction, the study of the $μ^+ μ^- \to b \bar b h$ process allows to enforce the stronger bounds on the Wilson coefficients of the $d=6$ operators. ### [130] [NNLO QCD Corrections to $D$-Wave Spin-Singlet Heavy Quarkonia Decay $η_{Q2}\toγγ$ via the Principle of Maximum Conformality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24455)
*Hua Zhou,Xing-Gang Wu,Qing Yu,Sheng-Quan Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在非相对论QCD有效理论框架下，对D波自旋单态重夸克偶素η_Q2→γγ衰变过程进行了直到NNLO QCD修正的全面研究，并采用最大共形性原理(PMC)消除了标度不确定性，给出了精确的衰变宽度和分支比预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始NNLO微扰级数存在显著的重整化与因子化标度不确定性，需要消除这种固有的标度歧义以获得可靠的物理预言。

Method: 基于非相对论QCD因子化形式，将总衰变宽度分解为微扰可算的短距离系数(SDCs)和非微扰的D波长距离矩阵元(LDMEs)。采用最大共形性原理(PMC)，递归应用重整化群方程处理α_s和D波LDMEs的跑动，得到有效强耦合常数α_s(Q_*)，从而消除标度依赖性。

Result: 确定的PMC标度为Q_*=1.483 GeV (η_c2)和Q_*=4.246 GeV (η_b2)。预言衰变宽度Γ_{η_c2→γγ}^{PMC}=3.322^{+0.899}_{-0.828} eV，Γ_{η_b2→γγ}^{PMC}=0.0188^{+0.0014}_{-0.0013} eV；分支比Br(η_c2→γγ)=(7.463^{+2.020}_{-1.860})×10^{-6}，Br(η_b2→γγ)=(6.460^{+0.481}_{-0.447})×10^{-7}。

Conclusion: PMC方法通过去除发散的重正子贡献，自然改善了SDCs微扰级数的收敛性，得到了标度不变的微扰级数，提供了更可靠的D波重夸克偶素双光子衰变理论预言。

Abstract: In this paper, we perform a comprehensive study of the decay process $η_{Q2}\toγγ$ for $D$-wave spin-singlet heavy quarkonia up to next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) QCD corrections within the nonrelativistic QCD effective theory. Following its factorization formalism, the total decay width is decomposed into perturbatively calculable short-distance coefficients (SDCs) and nonperturbative $D$-wave long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs). The original NNLO series of SDCs suffers from sizable renormalization and factorization scale uncertainties. To eliminate such inherent scale ambiguities, we adopt the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC). We show that recursively applying the renormalization group equations for the running of $α_s$ and $D$-wave LDMEs within the PMC framework yields an effective strong coupling $α_s(Q_\ast)$ consistent with the expansion coefficients, resulting in a scale-invariant perturbative series. The determined PMC scales are $Q_\ast=1.483$ GeV for $η_{c2}$ and $Q_\ast=4.246$ GeV for $η_{b2}$. By removing divergent renormalon contributions, the PMC naturally improves the convergence of the perturbative series for SDCs. Our PMC predictions for the total decay widths are $Γ_{η_{c2}\toγγ}^{\rm PMC} = 3.322^{+0.899}_{-0.828}\ \text{eV}$ and $Γ_{η_{b2}\toγγ}^{\rm PMC} = 0.0188^{+0.0014}_{-0.0013}\ \text{eV}$. The uncertainties arise from variations of the charm and bottom quark masses $Δm_c=\pm 0.07$ GeV, $Δm_b=\pm 0.06$ GeV, as well as systematic errors from uncalculated higher-order corrections. The corresponding branching ratios are $\text{Br}(η_{c2}\toγγ) = \big(7.463^{+2.020}_{-1.860}\big)\times 10^{-6}$ and $\text{Br}(η_{b2}\toγγ) = \big(6.460^{+0.481}_{-0.447}\big)\times 10^{-7}$.

Abstract: We study how the renormalization group running beta functions of mixing angles and leptonic CP phases affect the slow and fast oscillation modes at JUNO. On the other hand, the fast mode also receives corrections from the beta functions of the Dirac CP phase $δ_D$ and the Majorana CP phase $δ_{\rm M3}$. Since the fast mode is essentially the one measuring the neutrino mass ordering, the RG running effect can then interfere to deteriorate the sensitivity. Fortunately, the JUNO-TAO near detector can provide supplementary measurements of the RG running parameters to restore the mass ordering sensitivity.

### [135] [Analytic electromagnetic signatures of compact pentaquark structure: A multi-current QCD light-cone sum rules analysis of the $P_{ψs}^Λ$ states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24582)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所提出的两个特征信号（轻夸克比值-2和粲夸克贡献消零）不依赖于态-流配对，为验证紧致五夸克图像提供了可检验的判据，同时为区分不同结构模型提供了LCSR框架内的直接对比手段。

Abstract: Probing the internal organization of hidden-charm pentaquarks -- including the spin-color correlations that distinguish compact diquark-diquark-antiquark configurations from loosely bound hadronic molecules -- requires observables beyond mass spectroscopy. We argue that multi-current QCD light-cone sum rules (LCSR) provide a diagnostic framework through exact analytic relations among flavor-sector contributions enforced by the algebra of the interpolating currents. We identify two such signatures: (i) the light-quark contributions satisfy $μ_{u}/μ_{d}=e_{u}/e_{d}=-2$ in all four currents considered, reflecting a common Lorentz-color kernel; and (ii) for the $J_{3}(x)$ current the charm contribution vanishes identically, $μ_{c}=0$, from the Dirac structure of the anti-charm coupling rather than the pseudoscalar charm-diquark embedding alone. These predictions are paired with the $P_{ψs}^Λ(4338)$ and $P_{ψs}^Λ(4459)$ on mass grounds as a working hypothesis, since the $\pm 0.11~\text{GeV}$ uncertainties accommodate either state within $1σ$ of all four currents. The magnitudes $|μ|\sim 1$-$3\,μ_{N}$ lie above quark-model and heavy pentaquark chiral perturbation theory expectations ($|μ|\lesssim 0.5\,μ_{N}$). Applying the same procedure to two previous molecular LCSR analyses yields $μ_{u}/μ_{d}=-1/2$ rather than $-2$, providing an LCSR-internal contrast at the flavor-decomposed level even when total magnitudes are comparable. The two signatures are immune to the state-to-current pairing and offer falsifiable tests of the compact picture.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用重整化群过程，在耦合常数二阶下对有效粒子进行处理；引入小胶子质量调控红外奇异性；通过计算有效哈密顿量的矩阵元确定必要的抵消项；截断零模，并在紫外重整化后考察胶子质量趋于零时的极限行为。

Result: 自能项与胶子交换项之间的耦合产生了正比于SU(3)二次Casimir算符乘以胶子质量对数的项。色非单态子空间的矩阵元对数发散，而色单态子空间中由于Casimir算符为零，矩阵元有限。

Conclusion: 所构造的有效哈密顿量是Fock空间稠密子空间上良定义的对称形式，且适用于经典或量子计算机上的非微扰数值计算。

Abstract: The effective Hamiltonian of quantum chromodynamics in the front form of Hamiltonian dynamics is calculated and renormalized. The renormalization group procedure for effective particles up to the second order in the coupling constant is used. Small gluon mass is used to regulate infrared singularities of the theory. The counterterms necessary to renormalize the theory are determined by computing matrix elements of the effective Hamiltonian. The effective Hamiltonians are well-defined symmetric forms on a dense subspace of the Fock space. The zero modes are cut off but, once ultraviolet renormalization is performed, no divergences are found in the color singlet subspace in the limit of the gluon mass approaching zero. A major result is that the interplay between self-energy terms and gluon exchange effective terms generates a term proportional to the quadratic SU(3) Casimir operator times the logarithm of the gluon mass. Therefore, the matrix elements are logarithmically divergent in the color nonsinglet subspace, but finite in the color singlet subspace, because the Casimir operator vanishes in the color singlet subspace. The effective Hamiltonians are suitable for nonperturbative numerical calculations using either classical or quantum computers.

</details>


### [138] [From the Great Wave of Translation to the Force between Quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24052)
*Chris Quigg*

TL;DR: 本文从运河中偶然观测到的奇异行波出发，推导出Korteweg-de Vries（KdV）方程，该方程描述称为孤子的强鲁棒扰动。孤子对应一维薛定谔方程中无反射势的单束缚态，多个孤子组合可得到对称无反射势的多束缚态。KdV方程开创了求解束缚态集合逆散射问题的路径。将该形式应用于夸克偶素谱，可构建夸克间作用力的无反射近似禁闭势，并检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性。

Method: 以KdV方程描述的孤子现象为起点，利用孤子对应一维薛定谔方程无反射势且支持单一束缚态的特性，通过适当组合多个孤子构建对称无反射势以支持多个束缚态。借助KdV方程求解逆散射问题，并将该形式化方法应用于夸克偶素谱，构建无反射近似的禁闭势。

Result: KdV方程成功开辟了通过逆散射方法处理束缚态集合的路径；将该形式应用于夸克偶素谱，成功构建了描述夸克间作用力的无反射近似禁闭势，并可用于检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性。

Conclusion: 孤子理论（KdV方程）与量子力学的逆散射问题存在深刻联系，该联系不仅揭示了孤子的数学本质（无反射势的束缚态），还为夸克偶素谱分析提供了新的理论工具，可用于构建禁闭势并检验夸克间相互作用的味无关性。

Abstract: The chance observation of a novel traveling wave in a canal led over time to the formulation of a nonlinear wave equation -- the Korteweg--de Vries equation -- that describes strikingly robust disturbances now called solitons. The figure of an isolated soliton corresponds to a reflectionless potential that supports a single bound state in the one-dimensional Schrödinger equation. An appropriate combination of individual solitons yields a symmetric reflectionless potential that supports multiple bound states. Thus, the KdV equation opens the path to solving the inverse scattering problem for a collection of bound states. Applied to the quarkonium spectra, this formalism allows the construction of reflectionless approximations to the confining potentials that account for the force between quarks, and to tests of the flavor-independence of the interquark interaction.

Method: 提出基于事件级相对权重的方法，将参数变化的影响以权重形式映射到已生成的事件和分布上，从而避免了对不同参数配置进行重复模拟。

Abstract: We propose and validate a new method to trace the impact of parameter variations in the simulation of multi-parton interactions and colour reconnections in the Sherpa event generator. They are reflected, at an event-by-event basis, through relative weights with respect to the central production parameters that give rise to the generated events and distributions. Our method facilitates the tuning of the Monte Carlo event generator at a dramatically reduced computational cost, alleviates parameter sensitivity studies, and enables robust quantification of parametric uncertainties on-the-fly, one of the missing ingredients for future simulations of high-energy particle collisions. The method can easily be adapted to and implemented in other event generators. ### [141] [The $a_1(1420)$ in a Unitary Coupled-Channel Three-Body Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24709)
*Ajay S. Sakthivasan,Yuchuan Feng,Michael Döring,Maxim Mai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将三角形奇点机制嵌入到幺正三体振幅中，对COMPASS实验观测到的$\sqrt{s}\approx1.42$ GeV处具有$a_1$量子数的三π子能量增强现象进行拟合分析，结果表明该增强可由三角形奇点充分解释，无需引入额外的$a_1(1420)$极点，并同时提取了$a_1(1260)$共振参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: COMPASS实验在约1.42 GeV处观测到具有$a_1$量子数的三π子增强，最初归因于涉及$K^*(892)$、$K$和$\bar K$中间态的三角形奇点机制。然而，这一单圈过程仅构成更大耦合道框架中非对角跃迁的一部分。需要验证将该机制嵌入幺正三体振幅后能否自洽地描述实验线型，并判断该增强是否确实源于运动学奇点而非新共振。

Method: 将单圈三角形奇点计算嵌入到幺正三体振幅中，自洽地纳入末态相互作用及其显著效应。构建九道产生振幅，组合至$P$波等压线及所有子道同位旋，对COMPASS实验不同动量转移下的线型进行拟合。

Result: 拟合振幅成功在$\sqrt{s}\approx1.42$ GeV附近再现了$(πf_0)_P$道的窄增强结构。这表明三角形奇点机制足以解释观测到的增强现象，无需引入额外的真实$a_1(1420)$极点。此外，从数据中还提取了基态轴矢共振$a_1(1260)$的参数。

Conclusion: 三角形奇点机制可充分解释COMPASS实验中1.42 GeV处的增强信号，该增强并非来自新共振态$a_1(1420)$。同时，幺正三体振幅框架能有效处理此类运动学奇点效应与末态相互作用的耦合。

Abstract: An enhancement in the three-pion energy at around $\sqrt{s}\approx 1.42~\textrm{GeV}$ with $a_1$ quantum numbers was observed at the COMPASS experiment. This was later attributed to the triangle singularity mechanism involving an on-shell $K^*(892)$, $K$ and $\bar K$ intermediate states. The alignment of the decay $K$ with the spectator $\bar K$ produces an $f_0(980)$, resulting in a kinematic enhancement, which is classically explained by the Landau equations. However, this one-loop process forms only part of a non-diagonal transition in a much larger coupled-channel framework. This study demonstrates the feasibility of embedding one-loop triangle-singularity calculations into a unitary three-body amplitude allowing one to consistently incorporate final-state interactions and their potentially substantial effect. For this, up to $P$-wave isobars and all sub-channel isospins are combined in a nine-channel production amplitude that is fitted to COMPASS lineshapes at different momentum transfers. The fitted amplitude reproduces the narrow enhancement in the $(πf_0)_P$ channel near $\sqrt{s}\approx1.42$ GeV. This implies that the triangle singularity mechanism sufficiently explains the observed enhancement, and an additional genuine $a_1(1420)$ pole is not required. Incidentally, the parameters of the ground state axial vector resonance (the $a_1(1260)$) are also extracted from that data.

### [142] [Radiative decays of dynamically generated pentaquarks in the chiral unitary approach: the $P_c(4457)\to P_c(4312)\,γ$ transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24764)
*Ratirat Suntharawirat,Nongnaphat Ponkhuha,Daris Samart*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于手征幺正方法构建S波强子分子态，结合重夸克自旋对称性和局部规范相互作用。利用耦合道解的强耦合残差、重夸克自旋对称性确定电磁顶点（部分用朴素夸克模型估计），构建19个M1三角圈图，通过数值求积和闭合解析形式简化计算。引入软高斯形状因子考虑有限尺寸效应。

Result: 中心宽度6.7 keV，保守范围2-9 keV；$\bar D^{*0}\to\bar D^{0}γ$圈图为主导贡献；近阈值$\bar D^{*}Λ_c$圈图为主要修正；软形状因子使全宽降至约4 keV；级联衰变$Λ_b^{0}\to J/ψ\,p\,K^{-}γ$的辐射过程可被实验搜寻。

Conclusion: 该纯M1辐射衰变宽度对耦合道相对残差相位灵敏；宽度对结合能的依赖关系、与$P_c(4440)$辐射衰变的比值可作为检验五夸克态分子本性的关键观测量。

Abstract: We study the radiative decay of dynamically generated pentaquarks and apply the formalism to the transition $P_c(4457)(3/2^-)\to P_c(4312)(1/2^-)γ$. Both states are treated as $S$-wave hadronic molecules generated in the chiral unitary approach with heavy-quark spin symmetry and the local hidden gauge interaction. The photon therefore couples to the meson-baryon components of the two poles. The calculation combines the strong coupling residues of the coupled-channel solution, heavy-quark spin symmetry for the electromagnetic vertices, and a transverse assembly of the $M1$ triangle loops. A complete calculation gives nineteen triangle loops. We reduce each loop to a single numerical quadrature and give the closed analytic form. The electromagnetic vertices that are not fixed by data are estimated with the naive-quark model and heavy-quark spin symmetry. We normalize the main $D^*Dγ$ coupling to $\bar D^{*0}\to\bar D^{0}γ$ and test the same convention with $J/ψ\toη_cγ$. The central width is $6.7\keV$, with a conservative range of about $2$ to $9\keV$. This radiative decay process is a pure $M1$ transition with photon energy $143\MeV$. The $\bar D^{*0}\to\bar D^{0}γ$ loop gives the leading contribution. The near-threshold $\bar D^{*}Λ_c$ loop gives the main correction. A soft Gaussian form-factor on the leading diagram reduces the width to about $2\keV$, compatible with earlier molecular results, and decreases the full width to about $4\keV$. The coherent result is sensitive to the relative residue phases in the coupled-channel convention. We also estimate the cascade rate for $Λ_b^{0}\to J/ψ\,p\,K^{-}γ$ and discuss how the line can be searched for. The pure $M1$ content, the ratio to the $P_c(4440)$ radiative decay, and the binding-energy dependence of the width are proposed as tests of the molecular nature.

These excesses arise in final states containing leptons, missing transverse momentum, and associated $b$-jets, and motivate a search for a corresponding localized excess in the invariant-mass spectrum of the dilepton--photon system, $m_{\ell\ellγ}$, in events with associated $b$-jets. We use recent CMS measurements of the ${t\bar{t}}γ$ differential cross sections~\cite{CMS:2025zbe} to study the $m_{\ell\ellγ}$ spectrum and perform a search for a scalar-resonance contribution. ### [144] [Hyperon-pair spin tomography beyond scalar spin correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24811)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个过程无关的自旋层析成像框架用于Λ\barΛ对，揭示了STAR合作组已发表的标量关联P_{Λ\barΛ}存在连续密度矩阵简并性，仅靠标量迹无法判断纠缠。通过局域³P₀弦断裂基准模型，将STAR迹转化为可证伪的张量模式，并指出衰变馈入必须作为张量响应处理。在e⁺e⁻校准通道中，该基准预测Belle II运动学下各向异性A_C约0.3，需约10⁴对实现测量。纠缠声明需要完整的两自旋密度矩阵违反PPT判据。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 已发表的标量P_{Λ\barΛ}存在连续简并性：可分离张量补全和违反PPT判据的补全可具有相同迹。基准预测张量模式为C_⟂>0, C_∥<0, A_C>0。e⁺e⁻通道预测A_C约0.3（Belle II运动学），约需10⁴对测量。衰变馈入必须作为张量响应处理。

Conclusion: 纠缠声明需要完整的两自旋密度矩阵违反PPT判据，而非仅依赖标量迹。实验应测量完整的张量分量（横向、纵向及各向异性A_C）以获取不可约的纠缠证据。

Abstract: Spin correlations measured after hadronization probe how quantum information is transported through confinement. We formulate a process-independent spin-tomography framework for $Λ\barΛ$ pairs in which the weak-decay angles determine the full two-spin tensor rather than only its scalar trace. Applied to the short-range STAR correlation in unpolarized $pp\toΛ\barΛX$, the framework shows that the published scalar $P_{Λ\barΛ}$ leaves a continuous density-matrix degeneracy: separable tensor completions and completions that violate the positive-partial-transpose (PPT) criterion can have the same trace. The missing observables are the transverse and longitudinal tensor components and their anisotropy $A_C=C_\perp-C_\parallel$. A local ${}^{3}P_0$ string-breaking benchmark turns the STAR trace into the falsifiable pattern $C_\perp>0$, $C_\parallel<0$, and $A_C>0$. We further show that feed-down must be treated as a tensor response rather than as a universal scalar dilution. In the complementary $e^+e^-$ calibration channel, the same benchmark predicts a centrally enhanced $A_C$ of order $0.3$ in Belle II kinematics, measurable with about $10^4$ selected pairs for nominal spin-transfer parameters. A claim of entanglement requires the reconstructed two-spin density matrix, not the scalar trace alone, to violate the PPT bound.

### [145] [Probing Invisible Fermions in $B \to D^{*}\ell X_{\text{inv}}$ via Angular Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24865)

TL;DR: 本文研究了B→D*ℓX_inv半轻衰变，提出利用角分布观测来区分暗物质粒子（如惰性中微子）的质量和手征性，基于弱有效理论框架构建了敏感性可观测量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在一般弱有效理论框架下，作者系统研究了B→D*ℓX_inv衰变过程，其中X_inv代表质量不为零的不可见费米子。通过分析角分布中的结构变化，构建了对暗物质粒子质量敏感的可观测量，并区分了左手和右手轻子-暗扇区流。

Result: 发现暗物质费米子的质量会在角分布中引入独特的修正特征；识别出对暗物质粒子质量具有增强敏感性的可观测量；揭示了能够区分左手流与右手流轻子-暗扇区相互作用的角结构。

Abstract: Semileptonic decays $B \to D^{*} \ell X_{\text{inv}}$ provide a sensitive probe of light invisible particles, such as sterile neutrinos or dark-sector fermions. Within a general weak effective theory framework, we show that a massive invisible fermion induces distinctive modifications in the angular distributions. We identify observables with enhanced sensitivity to the invisible particle mass, allowing a clear discrimination of such scenarios, and highlight angular structures that differentiate left- and right-handed lepton-dark-sector currents.

### [146] [Symplectic non-Kähler manifolds with and without the Hard Lefschetz Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23996)
*Richard Hind,Adriano Tomassini*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文构造了无Kähler结构的紧流形，其上同时存在满足Hard Lefschetz条件（HLC）和不满足HLC的辛形式，且这些形式位于同一连通分支中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究辛形式与HLC之间关系的微妙性，特别是同一流形上不同辛形式是否满足HLC的连通性行为，以及无Kähler结构流形上HLC的存在性问题。

Method: 基于Fernández-Muñoz orbifold及其Cavalcanti-Fernández-Muñoz辛解消，构造单参数辛形式族；通过沿环面并集进行适当的辛爆破，得到一族辛流形，使得HLC在非零参数下成立而在中心参数处失效。

Conclusion: 展示了HLC与Kähler结构的独立性，揭示了辛拓扑中HLC的连通性行为的新现象，为辛几何与HLC的交互提供了新例子。

Abstract: In this paper we construct compact manifolds without Kähler structures that admit both a symplectic form satisfying the Hard Lefschetz Condition (HLC) and another symplectic form that does not. Our construction builds upon the orbifold introduced by Fernández and Muñoz and its symplectic resolution studied by Cavalcanti, Fernández, and Muñoz. By considering a one-parameter family of symplectic forms on the orbifold, we show that the corresponding resolved manifolds fail to satisfy the HLC for all parameters. However, after performing a suitable symplectic blowup along a union of tori, we obtain a family of symplectic manifolds for which the HLC holds for all non-zero parameters but fails at the central parameter. As a consequence, we exhibit a smooth manifold with no Kähler structure whose space of symplectic forms contains both HLC and non-HLC structures in the same connected component. This provides new examples of the subtle interplay between symplectic topology and the Hard Lefschetz property.

We consider a crepant resolution $X\to\mathbb{C}^2/\mathbb{Z}_{n+1}$ of the $A_n$-singularity, whose mirror $\check{X}$ is also realized as a resolution of $\mathbb{C}^2/\mathbb{Z}_{n+1}$. For each level $k\in\mathbb{Z}_{>0}$, we construct a space filling coisotropic A-brane $\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)}$ of $(X,kω)$ and determine its mirror B-brane $\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)}$ via fiberwise geometric quantization. We then define the endomorphism algebra $Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})$ by gluing analytic quantum tori using wall-crossing formulas and establish a mirror isomorphism $Hom_A(\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)},\mathcal{B}_{cc}^{(k)})\cong Hom_B(\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)},\check{\mathcal{B}}_{cc}^{(k)})$.

Even though in some cases, such as dimension $4$, there is a classification of the local normal forms, it can be a challenge to determine them explicitly. Our goal in this paper is to introduce techniques to compute information about these local normal forms. We then explain how this is useful for instance to study the $p$-coupled angular momentum. The techniques we introduce cover all cases in dimension $4$ and require solving biquadratic equations. Along the way we define two new notions: almost eigenvectors and aligned symplectic coordinates. They are useful to prove our results but also of independent interest. The proofs use our previous classification of normal forms and rely on a combination of analytic estimates and Galois theory of $p$-adic extension fields. ### [149] [On the temperature dependence of quasinormal modes in SYK and holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22679)

Abstract: It was recently found that the quasinormal modes (or Ruelle--Pollicott resonances) of the SYK model at infinite temperature form a Christmas tree shape, reminiscent of AdS black holes. We generalise this computation to finite temperature, allowing us to continuously connect the infinite temperature results to the low temperature regime dual to JT gravity. We contrast the movement of the quasinormal modes with a few examples: various AdS black holes, dynamical phase transitions, and the large $p$ SYK chain. We find that the relaxation rate increases monotonically with temperature only at strong coupling, corresponding to the gravitational regime. Byproducts of our investigations are new results on operator growth that may be of independent interest.
