### [150] [On the amplitude expansion of gluon correlators in $\textrm{AdS}_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23776)
*Humberto Gomez,Renann Lipinski Jusinskas,Arthur Lipstein,Cristhiam Lopez-Arcos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现 AdS₄ 中的树级胶子关联函数可以自然地展开为平空间散射振幅之和：每个 n 点关联函数可分解为能量极点求和，其留数为平空间振幅，而曲率修正则由合并外部数据的低点振幅捕获。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 AdS 关联函数计算方法（如费曼图）复杂且缺乏透明度，本文旨在提供一种更优雅、更透明的替代方案，能够直接在完整关联函数层面而非单个费曼图层面进行计算。

Method: 通过 AdS 版本的 Berends-Giele 流递归定义外部极化数据的合并，将 n 点关联函数分解为能量极点求和（留数为平空间振幅），曲率修正由合并外部数据的低点振幅自然捕获。

Result: 建立了所有多重数的公式，并通过五点费曼图计算验证了该展开的正确性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种在完整关联函数层面计算 AdS 关联函数的优雅替代方案，相比传统方法更透明高效。

Abstract: We show that tree-level gluon correlators in $\textrm{AdS}_4$ admit a natural expansion in terms of flat-space scattering amplitudes at all multiplicities. In particular, every $n$-point correlator can be decomposed into a sum over energy poles whose residues are flat-space amplitudes. The $n$-point amplitude encodes the flat-space limit while curvature corrections are captured by lower-point amplitudes with merged external data. The merging of external polarizations is recursively defined via an AdS analogue of the Berends-Giele currents, giving rise to all-multiplicity formulae which we verify against Feynman diagram computations up to five points. Crucially, our approach works at the level of full correlators rather than individual diagrams, providing an elegant and transparent alternative to conventional approaches for computing correlators in anti-de Sitter space.

</details>


### [151] [Multi-dimensional chaos II: String scattering amplitudes, curve repulsion, and RMT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24490)
*Massimo Bianchi,Maurizio Firrotta,Jacob Sonnenschein,Dorin Weissman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现弦散射振幅中的角度依赖曲线间距比分布符合随机矩阵理论的Gaussian β-系综，其中散射角相关曲线收敛于GOE (β=1)，极化角相关曲线收敛于GUE (β=2)，并通过面积形状因子展示了混沌过程的下降、斜坡和平台特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多维混沌在高激发态弦散射振幅中的表现，探索弦理论中混沌现象的数学特征。

Method: 分析弦散射振幅对散射角和极化角的导数零点曲线，引入"面积本征值"概念，计算间距比分布并与RMT的Gaussian β-系综对比，计算面积形状因子。

Result: 间距比分布符合RMT预测：散射角曲线→GOE (β=1)，极化角曲线→GUE (β=2)；面积形状因子展现出下降、斜坡和平台区域，斜坡斜率与β值一致。

Conclusion: 弦散射振幅系统表现出典型混沌特征，且不同角度自由度对应不同的普适性类别，揭示了弦理论与随机矩阵理论之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Multi-dimensional chaos refers to processes described by erratic functions of several dynamical variables. In this letter we analyze the string scattering amplitudes of highly-excited states and ground states. We show that the amplitudes, which depend on a scattering angle and a polarization angle, are characterized by two sets of non-intersecting curves associated with the vanishing of the derivatives with respect to the angles. We introduce the notion of the "area eigenvalue" $A_n$ associated with the $n$-th curve. We compute the spacings $δ_{n}= A_{n+1}-A_n$ and their ratios $r_{n}=\frac{δ_{n+1}}{δ_n}$. We show that the distributions of the spacing ratios take the form of the RMT Gaussian $β$-ensembles. The curves associated with the scattering angle tend to converge to the Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble value of $β=1$ and those related to the polarization angle to the Gaussian Unitary Ensemble $β=2$. We also compute the ``areas form factor" associated with the areas and discover the regions of decline, ramp and plateau which characterize chaotic processes. The slope of the ramp seems to agree with the $β$ values extracted from the distribution of the spacing ratios.

</details>


### [152] [Controlled Chaos in 4D SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23785)
*Florent Baume,Atakan Çavuşoğlu,Vivek Chakrabhavi,Jonathan J. Heckman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过 orbifold 4D $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超 Yang-Mills 理论构建了一类 4D 超共形场论，其中算符混合由一维自旋链描述。通过调节边际耦合，系统从安德森局域化过渡到混沌谱，并通过能级统计（能级排斥、谱刚性、谱形状因子）诊断混沌。同时指出 Krylov 复杂度等其它诊断不一定可靠，并讨论了全息对偶中的多迹动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌动力学在物理系统中至关重要，但直接验证相互作用量子场论中混沌的出现十分困难。本文旨在构造一类可精确调控的场论模型，以研究混沌从可积到混沌的转变机制。

Method: 采用 4D $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM 理论的 orbifold 构造，得到一类 SCFT；利用算符混合的受控子扇区映射为一维自旋链（最近邻相互作用，耦合由边际耦合常数调节）；通过分析 dilatation 算符本征值的统计分布（能级排斥、谱刚性、谱形状因子）诊断混沌；同时对比 Krylov 复杂度等诊断的可靠性。

Result: 调节边际耦合可实现混沌谱，而一般情形下自旋链呈现安德森局域化；混沌诊断中能级统计方法有效，但 Krylov 复杂度等诊断不一定能忠实反映混沌信息；该结构对应弦论实现中的混沌台球。

Conclusion: 该构造提供了一个可控的场论框架来研究混沌与局域化的转变，并揭示了 Krylov 复杂度作为混沌诊断的局限性；全息对偶中需考虑多迹效应（自旋链的分裂与合并）。

Abstract: Chaotic dynamics play an important role in a number of physical systems. One of the qualitative hallmarks of this behavior is the appearance of a sufficiently "complex" spectrum of energy levels. This also makes it challenging to directly verify the onset of chaos in interacting quantum field theories. We present a class of 4D superconformal field theories (SCFTs) given by orbifolds of 4D $\mathcal{N} = 4$ Super Yang--Mills theory in which operator mixing in a controlled subsector is described by an effective spin chain in one spatial dimension with nearest neighbor interactions tuned by the marginal couplings of the SCFT. Tuning the marginal couplings results in a chaotic spectrum, while generically the spin chain exhibits Anderson localization. We diagnose the onset of chaos by analyzing the statistical distribution of eigenvalues of the dilatation operator, in particular properties such as eigenvalue level repulsion, spectral rigidity, and the spectral form factor. We also show that other diagnostics such as Krylov complexity sometimes do not faithfully capture this information. This structure defines a chaotic billiard in the target space of the stringy realization. We also comment on the large $N$ holographic dual description, where the controlled single spin chain approximation must be supplemented by multi-trace dynamics, i.e., the splitting and joining of multiple spin chains.

</details>

### [154] [Towards OSV in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23893)

Motivation: 建立3d N=2 SCFT中超对称指数（S^1×S^2上的配分函数）与挤压三球面配分函数之间的精确解析关系，从而在AdS/CFT对偶中联系渐近AdS_4黑洞配分函数与对偶场论的大N极限，类比OSV猜想在渐近平坦黑洞中的成功。

Method: 利用3d N=2 SCFT的超对称局域化方法，在Cardy-like极限（小S^1半径和大挤压参数）下通过鞍点近似推导出关系Z_{S^1×S^2} ∼ |Z_{S^3_b}|^2；类似方法也应用于拓扑扭缠指数与挤压球面配分函数的关系。

Result: 建立了超对称指数与挤压三球面配分函数之间的平方模关系，以及拓扑扭缠指数与挤压球面配分函数之间的类似关系；在M2-膜SCFT中通过大N超对称局域化结果进行了详细验证；将结果推广到5d SCFT及其对偶的AdS_6黑洞情形。

Conclusion: 该工作为3d N=2 SCFT提供了超对称指数与挤压球面配分函数之间的非平凡联系，在AdS/CFT框架下类似于OSV猜想，为理解渐近AdS_4黑洞的微观熵提供了新途径，并暗示了更一般维度下类似关系的存在。

Abstract: We use supersymmetric localization for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs to establish a relation of the form $Z_{S^1\times S^2} \sim |Z_{S^3_b}|^2$ between the superconformal index and the squashed three-sphere partition function. This applies to general 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs and is derived using a saddle point approximation in the Cardy-like limit of small $S^1$ radius and large squashing parameter. We also show a similar relation between the topologically twisted index and the squashed sphere partition function. In the context of holography our results lead to a relation between the partition function of supersymmetric asymptotically AdS$_4$ black holes and the large $N$ limit of $Z_{S^3_b}$ of the dual SCFT. Since the latter encodes the gauged supergravity prepotential, this result is akin to the OSV conjecture for asymptotically flat black holes. We confirm this relation in detail for SCFTs arising from M2-branes using recent large $N$ results from supersymmetric localization. We also briefly discuss a similar relation for 5d SCFTs and its implications for asymptotically AdS$_6$ black holes.

The deformation is a solvable analogue for the interpolation in the transposition coupling in the moduli space of the AdS3/CFT2 duality. On the boundary side of that correspondence, we analyze the scaling limit from the equivariant to the ordinary cohomology ring for the Hilbert scheme of points on the plane in terms of Jack symmetric polynomials. Abstract: Symmetric mass generation is the interaction-induced opening of a fermion gap without spontaneous symmetry breaking. The anomaly-free 3-4-5-0 model of Wang and Wen provides a minimal one-dimensional setting for this phenomenon, but a direct lattice realization faces two obstacles: fermion doubling for local chiral discretizations and perturbative irrelevance of the six-fermion gapping interaction. We address both obstacles. First, we formulate the model on a strictly one-dimensional tangent-fermion lattice, where a nonlocal hopping produces a single chiral branch without a mirror partner while retaining an efficient tensor-network representation. Second, we add a Hubbard-type density-density interaction (Luttinger parameter $K$) that reduces the scaling dimension of the 3-4-5-0 interaction from $5$ to $5K$, making it relevant for $K<2/5$. It is negative in the \(D=4\) and \(D=5\) backgrounds, so the portal weakly suppresses visible strip anisotropy. This has a holographic RG interpretation: the normalizable dark scalar is weighted toward the IR horizon, while narrow strips probe the UV near-boundary RT region.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索着色扭结多项式在双尺度准经典极限下的不同相行为，理解量子A-多项式的分裂机制，以及双曲体积与经典A-多项式的关系。

Method: 通过分析对称着色Jones多项式满足的差分方程（量子A-多项式），在双尺度准经典极限（表示大小r ~ ℏ⁻¹）下，研究非齐次量子A-多项式的分裂，并用更多实例（不限于4₁扭结）进行说明。

Result: 发现存在两种不同相：一种经典作用量为零，另一种是双曲体积（扭结补空间在S³中的体积）的形变。非齐次量子A-多项式分裂为两部分；双曲体积仅是积分常数，在A-多项式方程中未被完全确定；经典A-多项式在L=1时与Alexander多项式成比例，但需满足非齐次量子𝒜-多项式的多项式性，可能意味着它并非最小形式。

Conclusion: 双曲体积在准经典形式下具有内在不确定性；经典A-多项式与Alexander多项式的比例关系需在非齐次量子𝒜-多项式框架下保持一致性，这对A-多项式的选取施加了约束。

Abstract: "Colored" knot polynomials satisfy difference equation w.r.t. the highest weights of the underlying representation -- which in the case of symmetrically colored Jones are named "quantum $A$-polynomials". In the double scaling quasiclassical (Kashaev) limit, when representation size $r\sim \hbar^{-1}$, there are different phases -- in one of them the classical action vanishes and in another one it is a deformation of hyperbolic volume (of a knot complement in $S^3$). This corresponds to a splitting of the non-homogeneous version of the quantum $A$-polynomial into two pieces, which we illustrate by more examples than just a figure-eight knot $4_1$ in the original paper. From the point of view of quasiclassics, hyperbolic volume is just an integration constant, which is not fully determined by the $A$-polynomial equation -- and actually remains ambiguous in this formalism. As a byproduct, we expect that classical $A$-polynomial at $L=1$ becomes proportional to Alexander: $A^{\cal K}(1,M)\sim Δ^{\cal K}(M)$ -- this seems true, but $A$ should be consistent with the polynomiality of {\it non-homogeneous quantum} ${\cal A}$-polynomial, what sometime implies that it is not minimal.

</details>
